\DoxyCodeLine{299     \textcolor{comment}{// Windows}}
\DoxyCodeLine{300     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Begin() = push window to the stack and start appending to it. End() = pop window from the stack.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{301     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Passing 'bool* p\_open != NULL' shows a window-\/closing widget in the upper-\/right corner of the window,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{302     \textcolor{comment}{//   which clicking will set the boolean to false when clicked.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{303     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ You may append multiple times to the same window during the same frame by calling Begin()/End() pairs multiple times.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{304     \textcolor{comment}{//   Some information such as 'flags' or 'p\_open' will only be considered by the first call to Begin().}}
\DoxyCodeLine{305     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Begin() return false to indicate the window is collapsed or fully clipped, so you may early out and omit submitting}}
\DoxyCodeLine{306     \textcolor{comment}{//   anything to the window. Always call a matching End() for each Begin() call, regardless of its return value!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{307     \textcolor{comment}{//   [Important: due to legacy reason, this is inconsistent with most other functions such as BeginMenu/EndMenu,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{308     \textcolor{comment}{//    BeginPopup/EndPopup, etc. where the EndXXX call should only be called if the corresponding BeginXXX function}}
\DoxyCodeLine{309     \textcolor{comment}{//    returned true. Begin and BeginChild are the only odd ones out. Will be fixed in a future update.]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{310     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Note that the bottom of window stack always contains a window called "{}Debug"{}.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{311     IMGUI\_API \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool}          Begin(\textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}* name, \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool}* p\_open = NULL, ImGuiWindowFlags flags = 0);}
\DoxyCodeLine{312     IMGUI\_API \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}          End();}
\DoxyCodeLine{313 }
\DoxyCodeLine{314     \textcolor{comment}{// Child Windows}}
\DoxyCodeLine{315     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Use child windows to begin into a self-\/contained independent scrolling/clipping regions within a host window. Child windows can embed their own child.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{316     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ For each independent axis of 'size': ==0.0f: use remaining host window size / >0.0f: fixed size / <0.0f: use remaining window size minus abs(size) / Each axis can use a different mode, e.g. ImVec2(0,400).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{317     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ BeginChild() returns false to indicate the window is collapsed or fully clipped, so you may early out and omit submitting anything to the window.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{318     \textcolor{comment}{//   Always call a matching EndChild() for each BeginChild() call, regardless of its return value.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{319     \textcolor{comment}{//   [Important: due to legacy reason, this is inconsistent with most other functions such as BeginMenu/EndMenu,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{320     \textcolor{comment}{//    BeginPopup/EndPopup, etc. where the EndXXX call should only be called if the corresponding BeginXXX function}}
\DoxyCodeLine{321     \textcolor{comment}{//    returned true. Begin and BeginChild are the only odd ones out. Will be fixed in a future update.]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{322     IMGUI\_API \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool}          BeginChild(\textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}* str\_id, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_vec2}{ImVec2}}\& size = \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_vec2}{ImVec2}}(0, 0), \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool} border = \textcolor{keyword}{false}, ImGuiWindowFlags flags = 0);}

\DoxyCodeLine{411     \textcolor{comment}{// Cursor / Layout}}
\DoxyCodeLine{412     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ By "{}cursor"{} we mean the current output position.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{413     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ The typical widget behavior is to output themselves at the current cursor position, then move the cursor one line down.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{414     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ You can call SameLine() between widgets to undo the last carriage return and output at the right of the preceding widget.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{415     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Attention! We currently have inconsistencies between window-\/local and absolute positions we will aim to fix with future API:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{416     \textcolor{comment}{//    Window-\/local coordinates:   SameLine(), GetCursorPos(), SetCursorPos(), GetCursorStartPos(), GetContentRegionMax(), GetWindowContentRegion*(), PushTextWrapPos()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{417     \textcolor{comment}{//    Absolute coordinate:        GetCursorScreenPos(), SetCursorScreenPos(), all ImDrawList:: functions.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{418     IMGUI\_API \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}          Separator();                                                    \textcolor{comment}{// separator, generally horizontal. inside a menu bar or in horizontal layout mode, this becomes a vertical separator.}}

X position given in window coordinates.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{442     \textcolor{comment}{// ID stack/scopes}}
\DoxyCodeLine{443     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Read the FAQ for more details about how ID are handled in dear imgui. If you are creating widgets in a loop you most}}
\DoxyCodeLine{444     \textcolor{comment}{//   likely want to push a unique identifier (e.g. object pointer, loop index) to uniquely differentiate them.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{445     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ The resulting ID are hashes of the entire stack.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{446     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ You can also use the "{}Label\#\#foobar"{} syntax within widget label to distinguish them from each others.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{447     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ In this header file we use the "{}label"{}/"{}name"{} terminology to denote a string that will be displayed and used as an ID,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{448     \textcolor{comment}{//   whereas "{}str\_id"{} denote a string that is only used as an ID and not normally displayed.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{449     IMGUI\_API \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}          PushID(\textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}* str\_id);                                     \textcolor{comment}{// push string into the ID stack (will hash string).}}

\DoxyCodeLine{499     \textcolor{comment}{// Widgets: Drag Sliders}}
\DoxyCodeLine{500     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ CTRL+Click on any drag box to turn them into an input box. Manually input values aren't clamped and can go off-\/bounds.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{501     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ For all the Float2/Float3/Float4/Int2/Int3/Int4 versions of every functions, note that a 'float v[X]' function argument is the same as 'float* v', the array syntax is just a way to document the number of elements that are expected to be accessible. You can pass address of your first element out of a contiguous set, e.g. \&myvector.x}}
\DoxyCodeLine{502     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Adjust format string to decorate the value with a prefix, a suffix, or adapt the editing and display precision e.g. "{}\%.3f"{} -\/> 1.234; "{}\%5.2f secs"{} -\/> 01.23 secs; "{}Biscuit: \%.0f"{} -\/> Biscuit: 1; etc.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{503     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Format string may also be set to NULL or use the default format ("{}\%f"{} or "{}\%d"{}).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{504     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Speed are per-\/pixel of mouse movement (v\_speed=0.2f: mouse needs to move by 5 pixels to increase value by 1). For gamepad/keyboard navigation, minimum speed is Max(v\_speed, minimum\_step\_at\_given\_precision).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{505     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Use v\_min < v\_max to clamp edits to given limits. Note that CTRL+Click manual input can override those limits.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{506     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Use v\_max = FLT\_MAX / INT\_MAX etc to avoid clamping to a maximum, same with v\_min = -\/FLT\_MAX / INT\_MIN to avoid clamping to a minimum.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{507     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ We use the same sets of flags for DragXXX() and SliderXXX() functions as the features are the same and it makes it easier to swap them.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{508     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Legacy: Pre-\/1.78 there are DragXXX() function signatures that takes a final `float power=1.0f' argument instead of the `ImGuiSliderFlags flags=0' argument.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{509     \textcolor{comment}{//   If you get a warning converting a float to ImGuiSliderFlags, read https://github.com/ocornut/imgui/issues/3361}}
\DoxyCodeLine{510     IMGUI\_API \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool}          DragFloat(const \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}* label, \textcolor{keywordtype}{float}* v, \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} v\_speed = 1.0f, \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} v\_min = 0.0f, \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} v\_max = 0.0f, const \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}* format = "{}\%.3f"{}, ImGuiSliderFlags flags = 0);     \textcolor{comment}{// If v\_min >= v\_max we have no bound}}

\DoxyCodeLine{643     \textcolor{comment}{// Popups, Modals}}
\DoxyCodeLine{644     \textcolor{comment}{//  -\/ They block normal mouse hovering detection (and therefore most mouse interactions) behind them.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{645     \textcolor{comment}{//  -\/ If not modal: they can be closed by clicking anywhere outside them, or by pressing ESCAPE.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{646     \textcolor{comment}{//  -\/ Their visibility state (\string~bool) is held internally instead of being held by the programmer as we are used to with regular Begin*() calls.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{647     \textcolor{comment}{//  -\/ The 3 properties above are related: we need to retain popup visibility state in the library because popups may be closed as any time.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{648     \textcolor{comment}{//  -\/ You can bypass the hovering restriction by using ImGuiHoveredFlags\_AllowWhenBlockedByPopup when calling IsItemHovered() or IsWindowHovered().}}
\DoxyCodeLine{649     \textcolor{comment}{//  -\/ IMPORTANT: Popup identifiers are relative to the current ID stack, so OpenPopup and BeginPopup generally needs to be at the same level of the stack.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{650     \textcolor{comment}{//    This is sometimes leading to confusing mistakes. May rework this in the future.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{651     \textcolor{comment}{// Popups: begin/end functions}}
\DoxyCodeLine{652     \textcolor{comment}{//  -\/ BeginPopup(): query popup state, if open start appending into the window. Call EndPopup() afterwards. ImGuiWindowFlags are forwarded to the window.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{653     \textcolor{comment}{//  -\/ BeginPopupModal(): block every interactions behind the window, cannot be closed by user, add a dimming background, has a title bar.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{654     IMGUI\_API \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool}          BeginPopup(const \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}* str\_id, ImGuiWindowFlags flags = 0);                         \textcolor{comment}{// return true if the popup is open, and you can start outputting to it.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{655     IMGUI\_API \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool}          BeginPopupModal(const \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}* name, \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool}* p\_open = NULL, ImGuiWindowFlags flags = 0); \textcolor{comment}{// return true if the modal is open, and you can start outputting to it.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{656     IMGUI\_API \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}          EndPopup();                                                                         \textcolor{comment}{// only call EndPopup() if BeginPopupXXX() returns true!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{657     \textcolor{comment}{// Popups: open/close functions}}
\DoxyCodeLine{658     \textcolor{comment}{//  -\/ OpenPopup(): set popup state to open. ImGuiPopupFlags are available for opening options.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{659     \textcolor{comment}{//  -\/ If not modal: they can be closed by clicking anywhere outside them, or by pressing ESCAPE.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{660     \textcolor{comment}{//  -\/ CloseCurrentPopup(): use inside the BeginPopup()/EndPopup() scope to close manually.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{661     \textcolor{comment}{//  -\/ CloseCurrentPopup() is called by default by Selectable()/MenuItem() when activated (FIXME: need some options).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{662     \textcolor{comment}{//  -\/ Use ImGuiPopupFlags\_NoOpenOverExistingPopup to avoid opening a popup if there's already one at the same level. This is equivalent to e.g. testing for !IsAnyPopupOpen() prior to OpenPopup().}}
\DoxyCodeLine{663     IMGUI\_API \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}          OpenPopup(const \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}* str\_id, ImGuiPopupFlags popup\_flags = 0);                     \textcolor{comment}{// call to mark popup as open (don't call every frame!).}}

\DoxyCodeLine{679 }
\DoxyCodeLine{680     \textcolor{comment}{// Tables}}
\DoxyCodeLine{681     \textcolor{comment}{// [BETA API] API may evolve slightly! If you use this, please update to the next version when it comes out!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{682     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Full-\/featured replacement for old Columns API.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{683     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ See Demo-\/>Tables for demo code.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{684     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ See top of imgui\_tables.cpp for general commentary.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{685     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ See ImGuiTableFlags\_ and ImGuiTableColumnFlags\_ enums for a description of available flags.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{686     \textcolor{comment}{// The typical call flow is:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{687     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ 1. Call BeginTable().}}
\DoxyCodeLine{688     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ 2. Optionally call TableSetupColumn() to submit column name/flags/defaults.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{689     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ 3. Optionally call TableSetupScrollFreeze() to request scroll freezing of columns/rows.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{690     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ 4. Optionally call TableHeadersRow() to submit a header row. Names are pulled from TableSetupColumn() data.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{691     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ 5. Populate contents:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{692     \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ In most situations you can use TableNextRow() + TableSetColumnIndex(N) to start appending into a column.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{693     \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ If you are using tables as a sort of grid, where every columns is holding the same type of contents,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{694     \textcolor{comment}{//      you may prefer using TableNextColumn() instead of TableNextRow() + TableSetColumnIndex().}}
\DoxyCodeLine{695     \textcolor{comment}{//      TableNextColumn() will automatically wrap-\/around into the next row if needed.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{696     \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ IMPORTANT: Comparatively to the old Columns() API, we need to call TableNextColumn() for the first column!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{697     \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ Summary of possible call flow:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{698     \textcolor{comment}{//        -\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{699     \textcolor{comment}{//        TableNextRow() -\/> TableSetColumnIndex(0) -\/> Text("{}Hello 0"{}) -\/> TableSetColumnIndex(1) -\/> Text("{}Hello 1"{})  // OK}}
\DoxyCodeLine{700     \textcolor{comment}{//        TableNextRow() -\/> TableNextColumn()      -\/> Text("{}Hello 0"{}) -\/> TableNextColumn()      -\/> Text("{}Hello 1"{})  // OK}}
\DoxyCodeLine{701     \textcolor{comment}{//                          TableNextColumn()      -\/> Text("{}Hello 0"{}) -\/> TableNextColumn()      -\/> Text("{}Hello 1"{})  // OK: TableNextColumn() automatically gets to next row!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{702     \textcolor{comment}{//        TableNextRow()                           -\/> Text("{}Hello 0"{})                                               // Not OK! Missing TableSetColumnIndex() or TableNextColumn()! Text will not appear!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{703     \textcolor{comment}{//        -\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{704     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ 5. Call EndTable()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{705     IMGUI\_API \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool}          BeginTable(const \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}* str\_id, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} column, ImGuiTableFlags flags = 0, const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_vec2}{ImVec2}}\& outer\_size = \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_vec2}{ImVec2}}(0.0f, 0.0f), \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} inner\_width = 0.0f);}
\DoxyCodeLine{706     IMGUI\_API \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}          EndTable();                                 \textcolor{comment}{// only call EndTable() if BeginTable() returns true!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{707     IMGUI\_API \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}          TableNextRow(ImGuiTableRowFlags row\_flags = 0, \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} min\_row\_height = 0.0f); \textcolor{comment}{// append into the first cell of a new row.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{708     IMGUI\_API \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool}          TableNextColumn();                          \textcolor{comment}{// append into the next column (or first column of next row if currently in last column). Return true when column is visible.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{709     IMGUI\_API \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool}          TableSetColumnIndex(\textcolor{keywordtype}{int} column\_n);          \textcolor{comment}{// append into the specified column. Return true when column is visible.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{710     \textcolor{comment}{// Tables: Headers \& Columns declaration}}
\DoxyCodeLine{711     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Use TableSetupColumn() to specify label, resizing policy, default width/weight, id, various other flags etc.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{712     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Use TableHeadersRow() to create a header row and automatically submit a TableHeader() for each column.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{713     \textcolor{comment}{//   Headers are required to perform: reordering, sorting, and opening the context menu.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{714     \textcolor{comment}{//   The context menu can also be made available in columns body using ImGuiTableFlags\_ContextMenuInBody.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{715     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ You may manually submit headers using TableNextRow() + TableHeader() calls, but this is only useful in}}
\DoxyCodeLine{716     \textcolor{comment}{//   some advanced use cases (e.g. adding custom widgets in header row).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{717     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Use TableSetupScrollFreeze() to lock columns/rows so they stay visible when scrolled.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{718     IMGUI\_API \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}          TableSetupColumn(const \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}* label, ImGuiTableColumnFlags flags = 0, \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} init\_width\_or\_weight = 0.0f, ImGuiID user\_id = 0);}
\DoxyCodeLine{719     IMGUI\_API \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}          TableSetupScrollFreeze(\textcolor{keywordtype}{int} cols, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} rows); \textcolor{comment}{// lock columns/rows so they stay visible when scrolled.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{720     IMGUI\_API \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}          TableHeadersRow();                          \textcolor{comment}{// submit all headers cells based on data provided to TableSetupColumn() + submit context menu}}
\DoxyCodeLine{721     IMGUI\_API \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}          TableHeader(const \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}* label);             \textcolor{comment}{// submit one header cell manually (rarely used)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{722     \textcolor{comment}{// Tables: Sorting}}
\DoxyCodeLine{723     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Call TableGetSortSpecs() to retrieve latest sort specs for the table. NULL when not sorting.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{724     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ When 'SpecsDirty == true' you should sort your data. It will be true when sorting specs have changed}}
\DoxyCodeLine{725     \textcolor{comment}{//   since last call, or the first time. Make sure to set 'SpecsDirty = false' after sorting, else you may}}
\DoxyCodeLine{726     \textcolor{comment}{//   wastefully sort your data every frame!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{727     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Lifetime: don't hold on this pointer over multiple frames or past any subsequent call to BeginTable().}}
\DoxyCodeLine{728     IMGUI\_API \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_gui_table_sort_specs}{ImGuiTableSortSpecs}}*  TableGetSortSpecs();                        \textcolor{comment}{// get latest sort specs for the table (NULL if not sorting).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{729     \textcolor{comment}{// Tables: Miscellaneous functions}}
\DoxyCodeLine{730     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Functions args 'int column\_n' treat the default value of -\/1 as the same as passing the current column index.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{731     IMGUI\_API \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}                   TableGetColumnCount();                      \textcolor{comment}{// return number of columns (value passed to BeginTable)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{732     IMGUI\_API \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}                   TableGetColumnIndex();                      \textcolor{comment}{// return current column index.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{733     IMGUI\_API \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}                   TableGetRowIndex();                         \textcolor{comment}{// return current row index.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{734     IMGUI\_API const \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}*           TableGetColumnName(\textcolor{keywordtype}{int} column\_n = -\/1);      \textcolor{comment}{// return "{}"{} if column didn't have a name declared by TableSetupColumn(). Pass -\/1 to use current column.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{735     IMGUI\_API ImGuiTableColumnFlags TableGetColumnFlags(\textcolor{keywordtype}{int} column\_n = -\/1);     \textcolor{comment}{// return column flags so you can query their Enabled/Visible/Sorted/Hovered status flags. Pass -\/1 to use current column.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{736     IMGUI\_API \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}                  TableSetBgColor(ImGuiTableBgTarget target, ImU32 color, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} column\_n = -\/1);  \textcolor{comment}{// change the color of a cell, row, or column. See ImGuiTableBgTarget\_ flags for details.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{737 }

\DoxyCodeLine{758     \textcolor{comment}{// Docking}}
\DoxyCodeLine{759     \textcolor{comment}{// [BETA API] Enable with io.ConfigFlags |= ImGuiConfigFlags\_DockingEnable.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{760     \textcolor{comment}{// Note: You can use most Docking facilities without calling any API. You DO NOT need to call DockSpace() to use Docking!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{761     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ To dock windows: if io.ConfigDockingWithShift == false (default) drag window from their title bar.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{762     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ To dock windows: if io.ConfigDockingWithShift == true: hold SHIFT anywhere while moving windows.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{763     \textcolor{comment}{// About DockSpace:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{764     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Use DockSpace() to create an explicit dock node \_within\_ an existing window. See Docking demo for details.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{765     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ DockSpace() needs to be submitted \_before\_ any window they can host. If you use a dockspace, submit it early in your app.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{783     \textcolor{comment}{// Drag and Drop}}
\DoxyCodeLine{784     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ On source items, call BeginDragDropSource(), if it returns true also call SetDragDropPayload() + EndDragDropSource().}}
\DoxyCodeLine{785     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ On target candidates, call BeginDragDropTarget(), if it returns true also call AcceptDragDropPayload() + EndDragDropTarget().}}
\DoxyCodeLine{786     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ If you stop calling BeginDragDropSource() the payload is preserved however it won't have a preview tooltip (we currently display a fallback "{}..."{} tooltip, see \#1725)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{787     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ An item can be both drag source and drop target.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{788     IMGUI\_API \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool}          BeginDragDropSource(ImGuiDragDropFlags flags = 0);                                      \textcolor{comment}{// call after submitting an item which may be dragged. when this return true, you can call SetDragDropPayload() + EndDragDropSource()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{789     IMGUI\_API \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool}          SetDragDropPayload(const \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}* type, const \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}* data, \textcolor{keywordtype}{size\_t} sz, ImGuiCond cond = 0);  \textcolor{comment}{// type is a user defined string of maximum 32 characters. Strings starting with '\_' are reserved for dear imgui internal types. Data is copied and held by imgui.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{790     IMGUI\_API \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}          EndDragDropSource();                                                                    \textcolor{comment}{// only call EndDragDropSource() if BeginDragDropSource() returns true!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{791     IMGUI\_API \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool}                  BeginDragDropTarget();                                                          \textcolor{comment}{// call after submitting an item that may receive a payload. If this returns true, you can call AcceptDragDropPayload() + EndDragDropTarget()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{792     IMGUI\_API const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_gui_payload}{ImGuiPayload}}*   AcceptDragDropPayload(const \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}* type, ImGuiDragDropFlags flags = 0);          \textcolor{comment}{// accept contents of a given type. If ImGuiDragDropFlags\_AcceptBeforeDelivery is set you can peek into the payload before the mouse button is released.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{793     IMGUI\_API \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}                  EndDragDropTarget();                                                            \textcolor{comment}{// only call EndDragDropTarget() if BeginDragDropTarget() returns true!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{794     IMGUI\_API const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_gui_payload}{ImGuiPayload}}*   GetDragDropPayload();                                                           \textcolor{comment}{// peek directly into the current payload from anywhere. may return NULL. use ImGuiPayload::IsDataType() to test for the payload type.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{806     \textcolor{comment}{// Item/Widgets Utilities}}

Note that you may get false positives (some widgets such as Combo()/ListBox()/Selectable() will return true even when clicking an already selected item).}}

\DoxyCodeLine{825     IMGUI\_API \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}          SetItemAllowOverlap();                                              \textcolor{comment}{// allow last item to be overlapped by a subsequent item. sometimes useful with invisible buttons, selectables, etc. to catch unused area.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{826 }
\DoxyCodeLine{827     \textcolor{comment}{// Viewports}}
\DoxyCodeLine{828     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Currently represents the Platform Window created by the application which is hosting our Dear ImGui windows.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{829     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ In 'docking' branch with multi-\/viewport enabled, we extend this concept to have multiple active viewports.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{830     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ In the future we will extend this concept further to also represent Platform Monitor and support a "{}no main platform window"{} operation mode.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{930 \textcolor{comment}{// Flags for ImGui::Begin()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{931 enum ImGuiWindowFlags\_}
\DoxyCodeLine{932 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{933     ImGuiWindowFlags\_None                   = 0,}
\DoxyCodeLine{934     ImGuiWindowFlags\_NoTitleBar             = 1 << 0,   \textcolor{comment}{// Disable title-\/bar}}
\DoxyCodeLine{935     ImGuiWindowFlags\_NoResize               = 1 << 1,   \textcolor{comment}{// Disable user resizing with the lower-\/right grip}}
\DoxyCodeLine{936     ImGuiWindowFlags\_NoMove                 = 1 << 2,   \textcolor{comment}{// Disable user moving the window}}
\DoxyCodeLine{937     ImGuiWindowFlags\_NoScrollbar            = 1 << 3,   \textcolor{comment}{// Disable scrollbars (window can still scroll with mouse or programmatically)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{938     ImGuiWindowFlags\_NoScrollWithMouse      = 1 << 4,   \textcolor{comment}{// Disable user vertically scrolling with mouse wheel. On child window, mouse wheel will be forwarded to the parent unless NoScrollbar is also set.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{939     ImGuiWindowFlags\_NoCollapse             = 1 << 5,   \textcolor{comment}{// Disable user collapsing window by double-\/clicking on it. Also referred to as "{}window menu button"{} within a docking node.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{940     ImGuiWindowFlags\_AlwaysAutoResize       = 1 << 6,   \textcolor{comment}{// Resize every window to its content every frame}}
\DoxyCodeLine{941     ImGuiWindowFlags\_NoBackground           = 1 << 7,   \textcolor{comment}{// Disable drawing background color (WindowBg, etc.) and outside border. Similar as using SetNextWindowBgAlpha(0.0f).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{942     ImGuiWindowFlags\_NoSavedSettings        = 1 << 8,   \textcolor{comment}{// Never load/save settings in .ini file}}
\DoxyCodeLine{943     ImGuiWindowFlags\_NoMouseInputs          = 1 << 9,   \textcolor{comment}{// Disable catching mouse, hovering test with pass through.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{944     ImGuiWindowFlags\_MenuBar                = 1 << 10,  \textcolor{comment}{// Has a menu-\/bar}}
\DoxyCodeLine{945     ImGuiWindowFlags\_HorizontalScrollbar    = 1 << 11,  \textcolor{comment}{// Allow horizontal scrollbar to appear (off by default). You may use SetNextWindowContentSize(ImVec2(width,0.0f)); prior to calling Begin() to specify width. Read code in imgui\_demo in the "{}Horizontal Scrolling"{} section.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{946     ImGuiWindowFlags\_NoFocusOnAppearing     = 1 << 12,  \textcolor{comment}{// Disable taking focus when transitioning from hidden to visible state}}
\DoxyCodeLine{947     ImGuiWindowFlags\_NoBringToFrontOnFocus  = 1 << 13,  \textcolor{comment}{// Disable bringing window to front when taking focus (e.g. clicking on it or programmatically giving it focus)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{948     ImGuiWindowFlags\_AlwaysVerticalScrollbar= 1 << 14,  \textcolor{comment}{// Always show vertical scrollbar (even if ContentSize.y < Size.y)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{949     ImGuiWindowFlags\_AlwaysHorizontalScrollbar=1<< 15,  \textcolor{comment}{// Always show horizontal scrollbar (even if ContentSize.x < Size.x)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{950     ImGuiWindowFlags\_AlwaysUseWindowPadding = 1 << 16,  \textcolor{comment}{// Ensure child windows without border uses style.WindowPadding (ignored by default for non-\/bordered child windows, because more convenient)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{951     ImGuiWindowFlags\_NoNavInputs            = 1 << 18,  \textcolor{comment}{// No gamepad/keyboard navigation within the window}}
\DoxyCodeLine{952     ImGuiWindowFlags\_NoNavFocus             = 1 << 19,  \textcolor{comment}{// No focusing toward this window with gamepad/keyboard navigation (e.g. skipped by CTRL+TAB)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{953     ImGuiWindowFlags\_UnsavedDocument        = 1 << 20,  \textcolor{comment}{// Append '*' to title without affecting the ID, as a convenience to avoid using the \#\#\# operator. When used in a tab/docking context, tab is selected on closure and closure is deferred by one frame to allow code to cancel the closure (with a confirmation popup, etc.) without flicker.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{954     ImGuiWindowFlags\_NoDocking              = 1 << 21,  \textcolor{comment}{// Disable docking of this window}}
\DoxyCodeLine{955 }
\DoxyCodeLine{956     ImGuiWindowFlags\_NoNav                  = ImGuiWindowFlags\_NoNavInputs | ImGuiWindowFlags\_NoNavFocus,}
\DoxyCodeLine{957     ImGuiWindowFlags\_NoDecoration           = ImGuiWindowFlags\_NoTitleBar | ImGuiWindowFlags\_NoResize | ImGuiWindowFlags\_NoScrollbar | ImGuiWindowFlags\_NoCollapse,}
\DoxyCodeLine{958     ImGuiWindowFlags\_NoInputs               = ImGuiWindowFlags\_NoMouseInputs | ImGuiWindowFlags\_NoNavInputs | ImGuiWindowFlags\_NoNavFocus,}
\DoxyCodeLine{959 }
\DoxyCodeLine{960     \textcolor{comment}{// [Internal]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{961     ImGuiWindowFlags\_NavFlattened           = 1 << 23,  \textcolor{comment}{// [BETA] Allow gamepad/keyboard navigation to cross over parent border to this child (only use on child that have no scrolling!)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{962     ImGuiWindowFlags\_ChildWindow            = 1 << 24,  \textcolor{comment}{// Don't use! For internal use by BeginChild()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{963     ImGuiWindowFlags\_Tooltip                = 1 << 25,  \textcolor{comment}{// Don't use! For internal use by BeginTooltip()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{964     ImGuiWindowFlags\_Popup                  = 1 << 26,  \textcolor{comment}{// Don't use! For internal use by BeginPopup()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{965     ImGuiWindowFlags\_Modal                  = 1 << 27,  \textcolor{comment}{// Don't use! For internal use by BeginPopupModal()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{966     ImGuiWindowFlags\_ChildMenu              = 1 << 28,  \textcolor{comment}{// Don't use! For internal use by BeginMenu()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{967     ImGuiWindowFlags\_DockNodeHost           = 1 << 29   \textcolor{comment}{// Don't use! For internal use by Begin()/NewFrame()}}

Notify when the string wants to be resized (for string types which hold a cache of their Size). You will be provided a new BufSize in the callback and NEED to honor it. (see misc/cpp/imgui\_stdlib.h for an example of using this)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{996     ImGuiInputTextFlags\_CallbackEdit        = 1 << 19,  \textcolor{comment}{// Callback on any edit (note that InputText() already returns true on edit, the callback is useful mainly to manipulate the underlying buffer while focus is active)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{997     \textcolor{comment}{// [Internal]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{998     ImGuiInputTextFlags\_Multiline           = 1 << 20,  \textcolor{comment}{// For internal use by InputTextMultiline()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{999     ImGuiInputTextFlags\_NoMarkEdited        = 1 << 21   \textcolor{comment}{// For internal use by functions using InputText() before reformatting data}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1000 }

\DoxyCodeLine{1029 \textcolor{comment}{// Flags for OpenPopup*(), BeginPopupContext*(), IsPopupOpen() functions.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1030 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ To be backward compatible with older API which took an 'int mouse\_button = 1' argument, we need to treat}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1031 \textcolor{comment}{//   small flags values as a mouse button index, so we encode the mouse button in the first few bits of the flags.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1032 \textcolor{comment}{//   It is therefore guaranteed to be legal to pass a mouse button index in ImGuiPopupFlags.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1033 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ For the same reason, we exceptionally default the ImGuiPopupFlags argument of BeginPopupContextXXX functions to 1 instead of 0.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1034 \textcolor{comment}{//   IMPORTANT: because the default parameter is 1 (==ImGuiPopupFlags\_MouseButtonRight), if you rely on the default parameter}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1035 \textcolor{comment}{//   and want to another another flag, you need to pass in the ImGuiPopupFlags\_MouseButtonRight flag.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1036 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Multiple buttons currently cannot be combined/or-\/ed in those functions (we could allow it later).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1037 \textcolor{keyword}{enum} ImGuiPopupFlags\_}
\DoxyCodeLine{1038 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1039     ImGuiPopupFlags\_None                    = 0,}
\DoxyCodeLine{1040     ImGuiPopupFlags\_MouseButtonLeft         = 0,        \textcolor{comment}{// For BeginPopupContext*(): open on Left Mouse release. Guaranteed to always be == 0 (same as ImGuiMouseButton\_Left)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1041     ImGuiPopupFlags\_MouseButtonRight        = 1,        \textcolor{comment}{// For BeginPopupContext*(): open on Right Mouse release. Guaranteed to always be == 1 (same as ImGuiMouseButton\_Right)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1042     ImGuiPopupFlags\_MouseButtonMiddle       = 2,        \textcolor{comment}{// For BeginPopupContext*(): open on Middle Mouse release. Guaranteed to always be == 2 (same as ImGuiMouseButton\_Middle)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1043     ImGuiPopupFlags\_MouseButtonMask\_        = 0x1F,}
\DoxyCodeLine{1044     ImGuiPopupFlags\_MouseButtonDefault\_     = 1,}
\DoxyCodeLine{1045     ImGuiPopupFlags\_NoOpenOverExistingPopup = 1 << 5,   \textcolor{comment}{// For OpenPopup*(), BeginPopupContext*(): don't open if there's already a popup at the same level of the popup stack}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1046     ImGuiPopupFlags\_NoOpenOverItems         = 1 << 6,   \textcolor{comment}{// For BeginPopupContextWindow(): don't return true when hovering items, only when hovering empty space}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1047     ImGuiPopupFlags\_AnyPopupId              = 1 << 7,   \textcolor{comment}{// For IsPopupOpen(): ignore the ImGuiID parameter and test for any popup.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1048     ImGuiPopupFlags\_AnyPopupLevel           = 1 << 8,   \textcolor{comment}{// For IsPopupOpen(): search/test at any level of the popup stack (default test in the current level)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1049     ImGuiPopupFlags\_AnyPopup                = ImGuiPopupFlags\_AnyPopupId | ImGuiPopupFlags\_AnyPopupLevel}
\DoxyCodeLine{1050 \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{1051 }

\DoxyCodeLine{1107 \textcolor{comment}{// Flags for ImGui::BeginTable()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1108 \textcolor{comment}{// [BETA API] API may evolve slightly! If you use this, please update to the next version when it comes out!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1109 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Important! Sizing policies have complex and subtle side effects, more so than you would expect.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1110 \textcolor{comment}{//   Read comments/demos carefully + experiment with live demos to get acquainted with them.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1111 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ The DEFAULT sizing policies are:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1112 \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ Default to ImGuiTableFlags\_SizingFixedFit    if ScrollX is on, or if host window has ImGuiWindowFlags\_AlwaysAutoResize.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1113 \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ Default to ImGuiTableFlags\_SizingStretchSame if ScrollX is off.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1114 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ When ScrollX is off:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1115 \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ Table defaults to ImGuiTableFlags\_SizingStretchSame -\/> all Columns defaults to ImGuiTableColumnFlags\_WidthStretch with same weight.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1116 \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ Columns sizing policy allowed: Stretch (default), Fixed/Auto.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1117 \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ Fixed Columns will generally obtain their requested width (unless the table cannot fit them all).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1118 \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ Stretch Columns will share the remaining width.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1119 \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ Mixed Fixed/Stretch columns is possible but has various side-\/effects on resizing behaviors.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1120 \textcolor{comment}{//      The typical use of mixing sizing policies is: any number of LEADING Fixed columns, followed by one or two TRAILING Stretch columns.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1121 \textcolor{comment}{//      (this is because the visible order of columns have subtle but necessary effects on how they react to manual resizing).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1122 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ When ScrollX is on:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1123 \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ Table defaults to ImGuiTableFlags\_SizingFixedFit -\/> all Columns defaults to ImGuiTableColumnFlags\_WidthFixed}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1124 \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ Columns sizing policy allowed: Fixed/Auto mostly.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1125 \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ Fixed Columns can be enlarged as needed. Table will show an horizontal scrollbar if needed.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1126 \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ When using auto-\/resizing (non-\/resizable) fixed columns, querying the content width to use item right-\/alignment e.g. SetNextItemWidth(-\/FLT\_MIN) doesn't make sense, would create a feedback loop.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1127 \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ Using Stretch columns OFTEN DOES NOT MAKE SENSE if ScrollX is on, UNLESS you have specified a value for 'inner\_width' in BeginTable().}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1128 \textcolor{comment}{//      If you specify a value for 'inner\_width' then effectively the scrolling space is known and Stretch or mixed Fixed/Stretch columns become meaningful again.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1129 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Read on documentation at the top of imgui\_tables.cpp for details.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1130 \textcolor{keyword}{enum} ImGuiTableFlags\_}
\DoxyCodeLine{1131 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1132     \textcolor{comment}{// Features}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1133     ImGuiTableFlags\_None                       = 0,}
\DoxyCodeLine{1134     ImGuiTableFlags\_Resizable                  = 1 << 0,   \textcolor{comment}{// Enable resizing columns.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1135     ImGuiTableFlags\_Reorderable                = 1 << 1,   \textcolor{comment}{// Enable reordering columns in header row (need calling TableSetupColumn() + TableHeadersRow() to display headers)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1136     ImGuiTableFlags\_Hideable                   = 1 << 2,   \textcolor{comment}{// Enable hiding/disabling columns in context menu.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1137     ImGuiTableFlags\_Sortable                   = 1 << 3,   \textcolor{comment}{// Enable sorting. Call TableGetSortSpecs() to obtain sort specs. Also see ImGuiTableFlags\_SortMulti and ImGuiTableFlags\_SortTristate.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1138     ImGuiTableFlags\_NoSavedSettings            = 1 << 4,   \textcolor{comment}{// Disable persisting columns order, width and sort settings in the .ini file.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1139     ImGuiTableFlags\_ContextMenuInBody          = 1 << 5,   \textcolor{comment}{// Right-\/click on columns body/contents will display table context menu. By default it is available in TableHeadersRow().}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1140     \textcolor{comment}{// Decorations}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1141     ImGuiTableFlags\_RowBg                      = 1 << 6,   \textcolor{comment}{// Set each RowBg color with ImGuiCol\_TableRowBg or ImGuiCol\_TableRowBgAlt (equivalent of calling TableSetBgColor with ImGuiTableBgFlags\_RowBg0 on each row manually)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1142     ImGuiTableFlags\_BordersInnerH              = 1 << 7,   \textcolor{comment}{// Draw horizontal borders between rows.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1143     ImGuiTableFlags\_BordersOuterH              = 1 << 8,   \textcolor{comment}{// Draw horizontal borders at the top and bottom.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1144     ImGuiTableFlags\_BordersInnerV              = 1 << 9,   \textcolor{comment}{// Draw vertical borders between columns.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1145     ImGuiTableFlags\_BordersOuterV              = 1 << 10,  \textcolor{comment}{// Draw vertical borders on the left and right sides.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1146     ImGuiTableFlags\_BordersH                   = ImGuiTableFlags\_BordersInnerH | ImGuiTableFlags\_BordersOuterH, \textcolor{comment}{// Draw horizontal borders.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1147     ImGuiTableFlags\_BordersV                   = ImGuiTableFlags\_BordersInnerV | ImGuiTableFlags\_BordersOuterV, \textcolor{comment}{// Draw vertical borders.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1148     ImGuiTableFlags\_BordersInner               = ImGuiTableFlags\_BordersInnerV | ImGuiTableFlags\_BordersInnerH, \textcolor{comment}{// Draw inner borders.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1149     ImGuiTableFlags\_BordersOuter               = ImGuiTableFlags\_BordersOuterV | ImGuiTableFlags\_BordersOuterH, \textcolor{comment}{// Draw outer borders.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1150     ImGuiTableFlags\_Borders                    = ImGuiTableFlags\_BordersInner | ImGuiTableFlags\_BordersOuter,   \textcolor{comment}{// Draw all borders.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1151     ImGuiTableFlags\_NoBordersInBody            = 1 << 11,  \textcolor{comment}{// [ALPHA] Disable vertical borders in columns Body (borders will always appears in Headers). -\/> May move to style}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1152     ImGuiTableFlags\_NoBordersInBodyUntilResize = 1 << 12,  \textcolor{comment}{// [ALPHA] Disable vertical borders in columns Body until hovered for resize (borders will always appears in Headers). -\/> May move to style}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1153     \textcolor{comment}{// Sizing Policy (read above for defaults)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1154     ImGuiTableFlags\_SizingFixedFit             = 1 << 13,  \textcolor{comment}{// Columns default to \_WidthFixed or \_WidthAuto (if resizable or not resizable), matching contents width.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1155     ImGuiTableFlags\_SizingFixedSame            = 2 << 13,  \textcolor{comment}{// Columns default to \_WidthFixed or \_WidthAuto (if resizable or not resizable), matching the maximum contents width of all columns. Implicitly enable ImGuiTableFlags\_NoKeepColumnsVisible.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1156     ImGuiTableFlags\_SizingStretchProp          = 3 << 13,  \textcolor{comment}{// Columns default to \_WidthStretch with default weights proportional to each columns contents widths.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1157     ImGuiTableFlags\_SizingStretchSame          = 4 << 13,  \textcolor{comment}{// Columns default to \_WidthStretch with default weights all equal, unless overridden by TableSetupColumn().}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1158     \textcolor{comment}{// Sizing Extra Options}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1159     ImGuiTableFlags\_NoHostExtendX              = 1 << 16,  \textcolor{comment}{// Make outer width auto-\/fit to columns, overriding outer\_size.x value. Only available when ScrollX/ScrollY are disabled and Stretch columns are not used.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1160     ImGuiTableFlags\_NoHostExtendY              = 1 << 17,  \textcolor{comment}{// Make outer height stop exactly at outer\_size.y (prevent auto-\/extending table past the limit). Only available when ScrollX/ScrollY are disabled. Data below the limit will be clipped and not visible.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1161     ImGuiTableFlags\_NoKeepColumnsVisible       = 1 << 18,  \textcolor{comment}{// Disable keeping column always minimally visible when ScrollX is off and table gets too small. Not recommended if columns are resizable.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1162     ImGuiTableFlags\_PreciseWidths              = 1 << 19,  \textcolor{comment}{// Disable distributing remainder width to stretched columns (width allocation on a 100-\/wide table with 3 columns: Without this flag: 33,33,34. With this flag: 33,33,33). With larger number of columns, resizing will appear to be less smooth.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1163     \textcolor{comment}{// Clipping}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1164     ImGuiTableFlags\_NoClip                     = 1 << 20,  \textcolor{comment}{// Disable clipping rectangle for every individual columns (reduce draw command count, items will be able to overflow into other columns). Generally incompatible with TableSetupScrollFreeze().}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1165     \textcolor{comment}{// Padding}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1166     ImGuiTableFlags\_PadOuterX                  = 1 << 21,  \textcolor{comment}{// Default if BordersOuterV is on. Enable outer-\/most padding. Generally desirable if you have headers.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1167     ImGuiTableFlags\_NoPadOuterX                = 1 << 22,  \textcolor{comment}{// Default if BordersOuterV is off. Disable outer-\/most padding.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1168     ImGuiTableFlags\_NoPadInnerX                = 1 << 23,  \textcolor{comment}{// Disable inner padding between columns (double inner padding if BordersOuterV is on, single inner padding if BordersOuterV is off).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1169     \textcolor{comment}{// Scrolling}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1170     ImGuiTableFlags\_ScrollX                    = 1 << 24,  \textcolor{comment}{// Enable horizontal scrolling. Require 'outer\_size' parameter of BeginTable() to specify the container size. Changes default sizing policy. Because this create a child window, ScrollY is currently generally recommended when using ScrollX.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1171     ImGuiTableFlags\_ScrollY                    = 1 << 25,  \textcolor{comment}{// Enable vertical scrolling. Require 'outer\_size' parameter of BeginTable() to specify the container size.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1172     \textcolor{comment}{// Sorting}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1173     ImGuiTableFlags\_SortMulti                  = 1 << 26,  \textcolor{comment}{// Hold shift when clicking headers to sort on multiple column. TableGetSortSpecs() may return specs where (SpecsCount > 1).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1174     ImGuiTableFlags\_SortTristate               = 1 << 27,  \textcolor{comment}{// Allow no sorting, disable default sorting. TableGetSortSpecs() may return specs where (SpecsCount == 0).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1175 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1176     \textcolor{comment}{// [Internal] Combinations and masks}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1177     ImGuiTableFlags\_SizingMask\_                = ImGuiTableFlags\_SizingFixedFit | ImGuiTableFlags\_SizingFixedSame | ImGuiTableFlags\_SizingStretchProp | ImGuiTableFlags\_SizingStretchSame}
\DoxyCodeLine{1178 }

\DoxyCodeLine{1233 \textcolor{comment}{// Enum for ImGui::TableSetBgColor()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1234 \textcolor{comment}{// Background colors are rendering in 3 layers:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1235 \textcolor{comment}{//  -\/ Layer 0: draw with RowBg0 color if set, otherwise draw with ColumnBg0 if set.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1236 \textcolor{comment}{//  -\/ Layer 1: draw with RowBg1 color if set, otherwise draw with ColumnBg1 if set.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1237 \textcolor{comment}{//  -\/ Layer 2: draw with CellBg color if set.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1238 \textcolor{comment}{// The purpose of the two row/columns layers is to let you decide if a background color changes should override or blend with the existing color.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1239 \textcolor{comment}{// When using ImGuiTableFlags\_RowBg on the table, each row has the RowBg0 color automatically set for odd/even rows.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1240 \textcolor{comment}{// If you set the color of RowBg0 target, your color will override the existing RowBg0 color.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1241 \textcolor{comment}{// If you set the color of RowBg1 or ColumnBg1 target, your color will blend over the RowBg0 color.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1242 \textcolor{keyword}{enum} ImGuiTableBgTarget\_}
\DoxyCodeLine{1243 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1244     ImGuiTableBgTarget\_None                         = 0,}
\DoxyCodeLine{1245     ImGuiTableBgTarget\_RowBg0                       = 1,        \textcolor{comment}{// Set row background color 0 (generally used for background, automatically set when ImGuiTableFlags\_RowBg is used)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1246     ImGuiTableBgTarget\_RowBg1                       = 2,        \textcolor{comment}{// Set row background color 1 (generally used for selection marking)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1247     ImGuiTableBgTarget\_CellBg                       = 3         \textcolor{comment}{// Set cell background color (top-\/most color)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1248 \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{1249 }

Important: If you are trying to tell how to dispatch your low-\/level inputs, do NOT use this. Use 'io.WantCaptureMouse' instead! Please read the FAQ!}}

This is extremely unusual within the dear imgui ecosystem and so we made it explicit.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{1423 \textcolor{comment}{// Configuration flags stored in io.ConfigFlags. Set by user/application.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1424 \textcolor{keyword}{enum} ImGuiConfigFlags\_}
\DoxyCodeLine{1425 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1426     ImGuiConfigFlags\_None                   = 0,}
\DoxyCodeLine{1427     ImGuiConfigFlags\_NavEnableKeyboard      = 1 << 0,   \textcolor{comment}{// Master keyboard navigation enable flag. NewFrame() will automatically fill io.NavInputs[] based on io.KeysDown[].}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1428     ImGuiConfigFlags\_NavEnableGamepad       = 1 << 1,   \textcolor{comment}{// Master gamepad navigation enable flag. This is mostly to instruct your imgui backend to fill io.NavInputs[]. Backend also needs to set ImGuiBackendFlags\_HasGamepad.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1429     ImGuiConfigFlags\_NavEnableSetMousePos   = 1 << 2,   \textcolor{comment}{// Instruct navigation to move the mouse cursor. May be useful on TV/console systems where moving a virtual mouse is awkward. Will update io.MousePos and set io.WantSetMousePos=true. If enabled you MUST honor io.WantSetMousePos requests in your backend, otherwise ImGui will react as if the mouse is jumping around back and forth.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1430     ImGuiConfigFlags\_NavNoCaptureKeyboard   = 1 << 3,   \textcolor{comment}{// Instruct navigation to not set the io.WantCaptureKeyboard flag when io.NavActive is set.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1431     ImGuiConfigFlags\_NoMouse                = 1 << 4,   \textcolor{comment}{// Instruct imgui to clear mouse position/buttons in NewFrame(). This allows ignoring the mouse information set by the backend.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1432     ImGuiConfigFlags\_NoMouseCursorChange    = 1 << 5,   \textcolor{comment}{// Instruct backend to not alter mouse cursor shape and visibility. Use if the backend cursor changes are interfering with yours and you don't want to use SetMouseCursor() to change mouse cursor. You may want to honor requests from imgui by reading GetMouseCursor() yourself instead.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1433 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1434     \textcolor{comment}{// [BETA] Docking}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1435     ImGuiConfigFlags\_DockingEnable          = 1 << 6,   \textcolor{comment}{// Docking enable flags.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1436 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1437     \textcolor{comment}{// [BETA] Viewports}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1438     \textcolor{comment}{// When using viewports it is recommended that your default value for ImGuiCol\_WindowBg is opaque (Alpha=1.0) so transition to a viewport won't be noticeable.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1439     ImGuiConfigFlags\_ViewportsEnable        = 1 << 10,  \textcolor{comment}{// Viewport enable flags (require both ImGuiBackendFlags\_PlatformHasViewports + ImGuiBackendFlags\_RendererHasViewports set by the respective backends)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1440     ImGuiConfigFlags\_DpiEnableScaleViewports= 1 << 14,  \textcolor{comment}{// [BETA: Don't use] FIXME-\/DPI: Reposition and resize imgui windows when the DpiScale of a viewport changed (mostly useful for the main viewport hosting other window). Note that resizing the main window itself is up to your application.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1441     ImGuiConfigFlags\_DpiEnableScaleFonts    = 1 << 15,  \textcolor{comment}{// [BETA: Don't use] FIXME-\/DPI: Request bitmap-\/scaled fonts to match DpiScale. This is a very low-\/quality workaround. The correct way to handle DPI is \_currently\_ to replace the atlas and/or fonts in the Platform\_OnChangedViewport callback, but this is all early work in progress.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1442 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1443     \textcolor{comment}{// User storage (to allow your backend/engine to communicate to code that may be shared between multiple projects. Those flags are not used by core Dear ImGui)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1444     ImGuiConfigFlags\_IsSRGB                 = 1 << 20,  \textcolor{comment}{// Application is SRGB-\/aware.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1445     ImGuiConfigFlags\_IsTouchScreen          = 1 << 21   \textcolor{comment}{// Application is using a touch screen instead of a mouse.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1446 \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{1447 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1448 \textcolor{comment}{// Backend capabilities flags stored in io.BackendFlags. Set by imgui\_impl\_xxx or custom backend.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1449 \textcolor{keyword}{enum} ImGuiBackendFlags\_}
\DoxyCodeLine{1450 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1451     ImGuiBackendFlags\_None                  = 0,}
\DoxyCodeLine{1452     ImGuiBackendFlags\_HasGamepad            = 1 << 0,   \textcolor{comment}{// Backend Platform supports gamepad and currently has one connected.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1453     ImGuiBackendFlags\_HasMouseCursors       = 1 << 1,   \textcolor{comment}{// Backend Platform supports honoring GetMouseCursor() value to change the OS cursor shape.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1454     ImGuiBackendFlags\_HasSetMousePos        = 1 << 2,   \textcolor{comment}{// Backend Platform supports io.WantSetMousePos requests to reposition the OS mouse position (only used if ImGuiConfigFlags\_NavEnableSetMousePos is set).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1455     ImGuiBackendFlags\_RendererHasVtxOffset  = 1 << 3,   \textcolor{comment}{// Backend Renderer supports ImDrawCmd::VtxOffset. This enables output of large meshes (64K+ vertices) while still using 16-\/bit indices.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1456 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1457     \textcolor{comment}{// [BETA] Viewports}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1458     ImGuiBackendFlags\_PlatformHasViewports  = 1 << 10,  \textcolor{comment}{// Backend Platform supports multiple viewports.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1459     ImGuiBackendFlags\_HasMouseHoveredViewport=1 << 11,  \textcolor{comment}{// Backend Platform supports setting io.MouseHoveredViewport to the viewport directly under the mouse \_IGNORING\_ viewports with the ImGuiViewportFlags\_NoInputs flag and \_REGARDLESS\_ of whether another viewport is focused and may be capturing the mouse. This information is \_NOT EASY\_ to provide correctly with most high-\/level engines! Don't set this without studying \_carefully\_ how the backends handle ImGuiViewportFlags\_NoInputs!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1460     ImGuiBackendFlags\_RendererHasViewports  = 1 << 12   \textcolor{comment}{// Backend Renderer supports multiple viewports.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1461 \};}

\DoxyCodeLine{1681 \textcolor{comment}{// IM\_MALLOC(), IM\_FREE(), IM\_NEW(), IM\_PLACEMENT\_NEW(), IM\_DELETE()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1682 \textcolor{comment}{// We call C++ constructor on own allocated memory via the placement "{}new(ptr) Type()"{} syntax.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1683 \textcolor{comment}{// Defining a custom placement new() with a custom parameter allows us to bypass including <new> which on some platforms complains when user has disabled exceptions.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{1696 \textcolor{comment}{// ImVector<>}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1697 \textcolor{comment}{// Lightweight std::vector<>-\/like class to avoid dragging dependencies (also, some implementations of STL with debug enabled are absurdly slow, we bypass it so our code runs fast in debug).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1698 \textcolor{comment}{//-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1699 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ You generally do NOT need to care or use this ever. But we need to make it available in imgui.h because some of our public structures are relying on it.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1700 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ We use std-\/like naming convention here, which is a little unusual for this codebase.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1701 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Important: clear() frees memory, resize(0) keep the allocated buffer. We use resize(0) a lot to intentionally recycle allocated buffers across frames and amortize our costs.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1702 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Important: our implementation does NOT call C++ constructors/destructors, we treat everything as raw data! This is intentional but be extra mindful of that,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1703 \textcolor{comment}{//   Do NOT use this class as a std::vector replacement in your own code! Many of the structures used by dear imgui can be safely initialized by a zero-\/memset.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1704 \textcolor{comment}{//-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1705 }

By default, viewports are marked with ParentViewportId = <main\_viewport>, expecting the platform backend to set\_appData a parent/child relationship between the OS windows (some backend may ignore this). Set to true if you want the default to be 0, then all viewports will be top-\/level OS windows.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{1968 \textcolor{comment}{// Shared state of InputText(), passed as an argument to your callback when a ImGuiInputTextFlags\_Callback* flag is used.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1969 \textcolor{comment}{// The callback function should return 0 by default.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1970 \textcolor{comment}{// Callbacks (follow a flag name and see comments in ImGuiInputTextFlags\_ declarations for more details)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1971 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ ImGuiInputTextFlags\_CallbackEdit:        Callback on buffer edit (note that InputText() already returns true on edit, the callback is useful mainly to manipulate the underlying buffer while focus is active)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1972 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ ImGuiInputTextFlags\_CallbackAlways:      Callback on each iteration}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1973 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ ImGuiInputTextFlags\_CallbackCompletion:  Callback on pressing TAB}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1974 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ ImGuiInputTextFlags\_CallbackHistory:     Callback on pressing Up/Down arrows}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1975 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ ImGuiInputTextFlags\_CallbackCharFilter:  Callback on character inputs to replace or discard them. Modify 'EventChar' to replace or discard, or return 1 in callback to discard.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1976 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ ImGuiInputTextFlags\_CallbackResize:      Callback on buffer capacity changes request (beyond 'buf\_size' parameter value), allowing the string to grow.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1977 \textcolor{keyword}{struct }\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_gui_input_text_callback_data}{ImGuiInputTextCallbackData}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1978 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1979     ImGuiInputTextFlags EventFlag;      \textcolor{comment}{// One ImGuiInputTextFlags\_Callback*    // Read-\/only}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1980     ImGuiInputTextFlags Flags;          \textcolor{comment}{// What user passed to InputText()      // Read-\/only}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1981     \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}*               UserData;       \textcolor{comment}{// What user passed to InputText()      // Read-\/only}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1982 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1983     \textcolor{comment}{// Arguments for the different callback events}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1984     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ To modify the text buffer in a callback, prefer using the InsertChars() / DeleteChars() function. InsertChars() will take care of calling the resize callback if necessary.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1985     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ If you know your edits are not going to resize the underlying buffer allocation, you may modify the contents of 'Buf[]' directly. You need to update 'BufTextLen' accordingly (0 <= BufTextLen < BufSize) and set 'BufDirty'' to true so InputText can update its internal state.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1986     ImWchar             EventChar;      \textcolor{comment}{// Character input                      // Read-\/write   // [CharFilter] Replace character with another one, or set to zero to drop. return 1 is equivalent to setting EventChar=0;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1987     ImGuiKey            EventKey;       \textcolor{comment}{// Key pressed (Up/Down/TAB)            // Read-\/only    // [Completion,History]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1988     \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}*               Buf;            \textcolor{comment}{// Text buffer                          // Read-\/write   // [Resize] Can replace pointer / [Completion,History,Always] Only write to pointed data, don't replace the actual pointer!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1989     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}                 BufTextLen;     \textcolor{comment}{// Text length (in bytes)               // Read-\/write   // [Resize,Completion,History,Always] Exclude zero-\/terminator storage. In C land: == strlen(some\_text), in C++ land: string.length()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1990     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}                 BufSize;        \textcolor{comment}{// Buffer size (in bytes) = capacity+1  // Read-\/only    // [Resize,Completion,History,Always] Include zero-\/terminator storage. In C land == ARRAYSIZE(my\_char\_array), in C++ land: string.capacity()+1}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1991     \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool}                BufDirty;       \textcolor{comment}{// Set if you modify Buf/BufTextLen!    // Write        // [Completion,History,Always]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1992     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}                 CursorPos;      \textcolor{comment}{//                                      // Read-\/write   // [Completion,History,Always]}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2152 \textcolor{comment}{// Helper: Key-\/>Value storage}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2153 \textcolor{comment}{// Typically you don't have to worry about this since a storage is held within each Window.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2154 \textcolor{comment}{// We use it to e.g. store collapse state for a tree (Int 0/1)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2155 \textcolor{comment}{// This is optimized for efficient lookup (dichotomy into a contiguous buffer) and rare insertion (typically tied to user interactions aka max once a frame)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2156 \textcolor{comment}{// You can use it as custom user storage for temporary values. Declare your own storage if, for example:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2157 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ You want to manipulate the open/close state of a particular sub-\/tree in your interface (tree node uses Int 0/1 to store their state).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2158 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ You want to store custom debug data easily without adding or editing structures in your code (probably not efficient, but convenient)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2159 \textcolor{comment}{// Types are NOT stored, so it is up to you to make sure your Key don't collide with different types.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2202 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2203 \textcolor{comment}{// Helper: Manually clip large list of items.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2204 \textcolor{comment}{// If you are submitting lots of evenly spaced items and you have a random access to the list, you can perform coarse}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2205 \textcolor{comment}{// clipping based on visibility to save yourself from processing those items at all.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2206 \textcolor{comment}{// The clipper calculates the range of visible items and advance the cursor to compensate for the non-\/visible items we have skipped.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2207 \textcolor{comment}{// (Dear ImGui already clip items based on their bounds but it needs to measure text size to do so, whereas manual coarse clipping before submission makes this cost and your own data fetching/submission cost almost null)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2208 \textcolor{comment}{// Usage:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2209 \textcolor{comment}{//   ImGuiListClipper clipper;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2210 \textcolor{comment}{//   clipper.Begin(1000);         // We have 1000 elements, evenly spaced.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2211 \textcolor{comment}{//   while (clipper.Step())}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2212 \textcolor{comment}{//       for (int i = clipper.DisplayStart; i < clipper.DisplayEnd; i++)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2213 \textcolor{comment}{//           ImGui::Text("{}line number \%d"{}, i);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2214 \textcolor{comment}{// Generally what happens is:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2215 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Clipper lets you process the first element (DisplayStart = 0, DisplayEnd = 1) regardless of it being visible or not.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2216 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ User code submit one element.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2217 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Clipper can measure the height of the first element}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2218 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Clipper calculate the actual range of elements to display based on the current clipping rectangle, position the cursor before the first visible element.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2219 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ User code submit visible elements.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2220 \textcolor{keyword}{struct }\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_gui_list_clipper}{ImGuiListClipper}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2221 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2222     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}     DisplayStart;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2223     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}     DisplayEnd;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2224 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2225     \textcolor{comment}{// [Internal]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2226     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}     ItemsCount;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2227     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}     StepNo;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2228     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}     ItemsFrozen;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2229     \textcolor{keywordtype}{float}   ItemsHeight;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2230     \textcolor{keywordtype}{float}   StartPosY;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2231 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2232     IMGUI\_API \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_gui_list_clipper}{ImGuiListClipper}}();}
\DoxyCodeLine{2233     IMGUI\_API \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_gui_list_clipper}{\string~ImGuiListClipper}}();}
\DoxyCodeLine{2234 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2235     \textcolor{comment}{// items\_count: Use INT\_MAX if you don't know how many items you have (in which case the cursor won't be advanced in the final step)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2236     \textcolor{comment}{// items\_height: Use -\/1.0f to be calculated automatically on first step. Otherwise pass in the distance between your items, typically GetTextLineHeightWithSpacing() or GetFrameHeightWithSpacing().}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2237     IMGUI\_API \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} Begin(\textcolor{keywordtype}{int} items\_count, \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} items\_height = -\/1.0f);  \textcolor{comment}{// Automatically called by constructor if you passed 'items\_count' or by Step() in Step 1.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2238     IMGUI\_API \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} End();                                               \textcolor{comment}{// Automatically called on the last call of Step() that returns false.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2239     IMGUI\_API \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool} Step();                                              \textcolor{comment}{// Call until it returns false. The DisplayStart/DisplayEnd fields will be set and you can process/draw those items.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2240 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2241 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifndef IMGUI\_DISABLE\_OBSOLETE\_FUNCTIONS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2242     \textcolor{keyword}{inline} \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_gui_list_clipper}{ImGuiListClipper}}(\textcolor{keywordtype}{int} items\_count, \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} items\_height = -\/1.0f) \{ memset(\textcolor{keyword}{this}, 0, \textcolor{keyword}{sizeof}(*\textcolor{keyword}{this})); ItemsCount = -\/1; Begin(items\_count, items\_height); \} \textcolor{comment}{// [removed in 1.79]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2243 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2244 \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{2245 }

\DoxyCodeLine{2257 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define IM\_COL32\_A\_SHIFT    24}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2259 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2260 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define IM\_COL32(R,G,B,A)    (((ImU32)(A)<<IM\_COL32\_A\_SHIFT) | ((ImU32)(B)<<IM\_COL32\_B\_SHIFT) | ((ImU32)(G)<<IM\_COL32\_G\_SHIFT) | ((ImU32)(R)<<IM\_COL32\_R\_SHIFT))}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2262 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define IM\_COL32\_BLACK       IM\_COL32(0,0,0,255)        }\textcolor{comment}{// Opaque black}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2263 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define IM\_COL32\_BLACK\_TRANS IM\_COL32(0,0,0,0)          }\textcolor{comment}{// Transparent black = 0x00000000}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2264 }

\DoxyCodeLine{2296 \textcolor{comment}{// ImDrawCallback: Draw callbacks for advanced uses [configurable type: override in imconfig.h]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2297 \textcolor{comment}{// NB: You most likely do NOT need to use draw callbacks just to create your own widget or customized UI rendering,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2298 \textcolor{comment}{// you can poke into the draw list for that! Draw callback may be useful for example to:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2299 \textcolor{comment}{//  A) Change your GPU render state,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2300 \textcolor{comment}{//  B) render a complex 3D scene inside a UI element without an intermediate texture/render target, etc.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2301 \textcolor{comment}{// The expected behavior from your rendering function is 'if (cmd.UserCallback != NULL) \{ cmd.UserCallback(parent\_list, cmd); \} else \{ RenderTriangles() \}'}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2302 \textcolor{comment}{// If you want to override the signature of ImDrawCallback, you can simply use e.g. '\#define ImDrawCallback MyDrawCallback' (in imconfig.h) + update rendering backend accordingly.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2303 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifndef ImDrawCallback}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2304 \textcolor{keyword}{typedef} void (*ImDrawCallback)(\textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_draw_list}{ImDrawList}}* parent\_list, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_draw_cmd}{ImDrawCmd}}* cmd);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2305 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2306 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2307 \textcolor{comment}{// Special Draw callback value to request renderer backend to reset the graphics/render state.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2308 \textcolor{comment}{// The renderer backend needs to handle this special value, otherwise it will crash trying to call a function at this address.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2309 \textcolor{comment}{// This is useful for example if you submitted callbacks which you know have altered the render state and you want it to be restored.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2310 \textcolor{comment}{// It is not done by default because they are many perfectly useful way of altering render state for imgui contents (e.g. changing shader/blending settings before an Image call).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2311 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define ImDrawCallback\_ResetRenderState     (ImDrawCallback)(-\/1)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2312 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2313 \textcolor{comment}{// Typically, 1 command = 1 GPU draw call (unless command is a callback)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2314 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ VtxOffset/IdxOffset: When 'io.BackendFlags \& ImGuiBackendFlags\_RendererHasVtxOffset' is enabled,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2315 \textcolor{comment}{//   those fields allow us to render meshes larger than 64K vertices while keeping 16-\/bit indices.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2316 \textcolor{comment}{//   Pre-\/1.71 backends will typically ignore the VtxOffset/IdxOffset fields.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2317 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ The ClipRect/TextureId/VtxOffset fields must be contiguous as we memcmp() them together (this is asserted for).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2318 \textcolor{keyword}{struct }\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_draw_cmd}{ImDrawCmd}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2319 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2320     \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_vec4}{ImVec4}}          ClipRect;           \textcolor{comment}{// 4*4  // Clipping rectangle (x1, y1, x2, y2). Subtract ImDrawData-\/>DisplayPos to get clipping rectangle in "{}viewport"{} coordinates}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2321     ImTextureID     TextureId;          \textcolor{comment}{// 4-\/8  // User-\/provided texture ID. Set by user in ImfontAtlas::SetTexID() for fonts or passed to Image*() functions. Ignore if never using images or multiple fonts atlas.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2322     \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}    VtxOffset;          \textcolor{comment}{// 4    // Start offset in vertex buffer. \DoxyCodeLine{2323     \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}    IdxOffset;          \textcolor{comment}{// 4    // Start offset in index buffer. Always equal to sum of ElemCount drawn so far.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2324     \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}    ElemCount;          \textcolor{comment}{// 4    // Number of indices (multiple of 3) to be rendered as triangles. Vertices are stored in the callee ImDrawList's vtx\_buffer[] array, indices in idx\_buffer[].}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2325     ImDrawCallback  UserCallback;       \textcolor{comment}{// 4-\/8  // If != NULL, call the function instead of rendering the vertices. clip\_rect and texture\_id will be set normally.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2326     \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}*           UserCallbackData;   \textcolor{comment}{// 4-\/8  // The draw callback code can access this.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2329 \};}

\DoxyCodeLine{2348 \textcolor{comment}{// The code expect ImVec2 pos (8 bytes), ImVec2 uv (8 bytes), ImU32 col (4 bytes), but you can re-\/order them or add other fields as needed to simplify integration in your engine.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2349 \textcolor{comment}{// The type has to be described within the macro (you can either declare the struct or use a typedef). This is because ImVec2/ImU32 are likely not declared a the time you'd want to set your type up.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2350 \textcolor{comment}{// NOTE: IMGUI DOESN'T CLEAR THE STRUCTURE AND DOESN'T CALL A CONSTRUCTOR SO ANY CUSTOM FIELD WILL BE UNINITIALIZED. IF YOU ADD EXTRA FIELDS (SUCH AS A 'Z' COORDINATES) YOU WILL NEED TO CLEAR THEM DURING RENDER OR TO IGNORE THEM.}}
