\DoxyCodeLine{2387 \textcolor{comment}{// Flags for ImDrawList functions}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2388 \textcolor{comment}{// (Legacy: bit 0 must always correspond to ImDrawFlags\_Closed to be backward compatible with old API using a bool. Bits 1..3 must be unused)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2389 \textcolor{keyword}{enum} ImDrawFlags\_}
\DoxyCodeLine{2390 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2391     ImDrawFlags\_None                        = 0,}
\DoxyCodeLine{2392     ImDrawFlags\_Closed                      = 1 << 0, \textcolor{comment}{// PathStroke(), AddPolyline(): specify that shape should be closed (Important: this is always == 1 for legacy reason)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2393     ImDrawFlags\_RoundCornersTopLeft         = 1 << 4, \textcolor{comment}{// AddRect(), AddRectFilled(), PathRect(): enable rounding top-\/left corner only (when rounding > 0.0f, we default to all corners). Was 0x01.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2394     ImDrawFlags\_RoundCornersTopRight        = 1 << 5, \textcolor{comment}{// AddRect(), AddRectFilled(), PathRect(): enable rounding top-\/right corner only (when rounding > 0.0f, we default to all corners). Was 0x02.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2395     ImDrawFlags\_RoundCornersBottomLeft      = 1 << 6, \textcolor{comment}{// AddRect(), AddRectFilled(), PathRect(): enable rounding bottom-\/left corner only (when rounding > 0.0f, we default to all corners). Was 0x04.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2396     ImDrawFlags\_RoundCornersBottomRight     = 1 << 7, \textcolor{comment}{// AddRect(), AddRectFilled(), PathRect(): enable rounding bottom-\/right corner only (when rounding > 0.0f, we default to all corners). Wax 0x08.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2397     ImDrawFlags\_RoundCornersNone            = 1 << 8, \textcolor{comment}{// AddRect(), AddRectFilled(), PathRect(): disable rounding on all corners (when rounding > 0.0f). This is NOT zero, NOT an implicit flag!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2398     ImDrawFlags\_RoundCornersTop             = ImDrawFlags\_RoundCornersTopLeft | ImDrawFlags\_RoundCornersTopRight,}
\DoxyCodeLine{2399     ImDrawFlags\_RoundCornersBottom          = ImDrawFlags\_RoundCornersBottomLeft | ImDrawFlags\_RoundCornersBottomRight,}
\DoxyCodeLine{2400     ImDrawFlags\_RoundCornersLeft            = ImDrawFlags\_RoundCornersBottomLeft | ImDrawFlags\_RoundCornersTopLeft,}
\DoxyCodeLine{2401     ImDrawFlags\_RoundCornersRight           = ImDrawFlags\_RoundCornersBottomRight | ImDrawFlags\_RoundCornersTopRight,}
\DoxyCodeLine{2402     ImDrawFlags\_RoundCornersAll             = ImDrawFlags\_RoundCornersTopLeft | ImDrawFlags\_RoundCornersTopRight | ImDrawFlags\_RoundCornersBottomLeft | ImDrawFlags\_RoundCornersBottomRight,}
\DoxyCodeLine{2403     ImDrawFlags\_RoundCornersDefault\_        = ImDrawFlags\_RoundCornersAll, \textcolor{comment}{// Default to ALL corners if none of the \_RoundCornersXX flags are specified.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2404     ImDrawFlags\_RoundCornersMask\_           = ImDrawFlags\_RoundCornersAll | ImDrawFlags\_RoundCornersNone}
\DoxyCodeLine{2405 \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{2406 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2407 \textcolor{comment}{// Flags for ImDrawList instance. Those are set automatically by ImGui:: functions from ImGuiIO settings, and generally not manipulated directly.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2408 \textcolor{comment}{// It is however possible to temporarily alter flags between calls to ImDrawList:: functions.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2409 \textcolor{keyword}{enum} ImDrawListFlags\_}
\DoxyCodeLine{2410 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2411     ImDrawListFlags\_None                    = 0,}
\DoxyCodeLine{2412     ImDrawListFlags\_AntiAliasedLines        = 1 << 0,  \textcolor{comment}{// Enable anti-\/aliased lines/borders (*2 the number of triangles for 1.0f wide line or lines thin enough to be drawn using textures, otherwise *3 the number of triangles)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2413     ImDrawListFlags\_AntiAliasedLinesUseTex  = 1 << 1,  \textcolor{comment}{// Enable anti-\/aliased lines/borders using textures when possible. Require backend to render with bilinear filtering.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2414     ImDrawListFlags\_AntiAliasedFill         = 1 << 2,  \textcolor{comment}{// Enable anti-\/aliased edge around filled shapes (rounded rectangles, circles).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2415     ImDrawListFlags\_AllowVtxOffset          = 1 << 3   \textcolor{comment}{// Can emit 'VtxOffset > 0' to allow large meshes. Set when 'ImGuiBackendFlags\_RendererHasVtxOffset' is enabled.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2416 \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{2417 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2418 \textcolor{comment}{// Draw command list}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2419 \textcolor{comment}{// This is the low-\/level list of polygons that ImGui:: functions are filling. At the end of the frame,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2420 \textcolor{comment}{// all command lists are passed to your ImGuiIO::RenderDrawListFn function for rendering.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2421 \textcolor{comment}{// Each dear imgui window contains its own ImDrawList. You can use ImGui::GetWindowDrawList() to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2422 \textcolor{comment}{// access the current window draw list and draw custom primitives.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2423 \textcolor{comment}{// You can interleave normal ImGui:: calls and adding primitives to the current draw list.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2424 \textcolor{comment}{// In single viewport mode, top-\/left is == GetMainViewport()-\/>Pos (generally 0,0), bottom-\/right is == GetMainViewport()-\/>Pos+Size (generally io.DisplaySize).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2425 \textcolor{comment}{// You are totally free to apply whatever transformation matrix to want to the data (depending on the use of the transformation you may want to apply it to ClipRect as well!)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2426 \textcolor{comment}{// Important: Primitives are always added to the list and not culled (culling is done at higher-\/level by ImGui:: functions), if you use this API a lot consider coarse culling your drawn objects.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2427 \textcolor{keyword}{struct }\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_draw_list}{ImDrawList}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2428 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2429     \textcolor{comment}{// This is what you have to render}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2430     \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_vector}{ImVector<ImDrawCmd>}}     CmdBuffer;          \textcolor{comment}{// Draw commands. Typically 1 command = 1 GPU draw call, unless the command is a callback.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2431     \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_vector}{ImVector<ImDrawIdx>}}     IdxBuffer;          \textcolor{comment}{// Index buffer. Each command consume ImDrawCmd::ElemCount of those}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2432     \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_vector}{ImVector<ImDrawVert>}}    VtxBuffer;          \textcolor{comment}{// Vertex buffer.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2433     ImDrawListFlags         Flags;              \textcolor{comment}{// Flags, you may poke into these to adjust anti-\/aliasing settings per-\/primitive.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2434 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2435     \textcolor{comment}{// [Internal, used while building lists]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2436     \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}            \_VtxCurrentIdx;     \textcolor{comment}{// [Internal] generally == VtxBuffer.Size unless we are past 64K vertices, in which case this gets reset to 0.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2437     \textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_draw_list_shared_data}{ImDrawListSharedData}}* \_Data;          \textcolor{comment}{// Pointer to shared draw data (you can use ImGui::GetDrawListSharedData() to get the one from current ImGui context)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2438     \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}*             \_OwnerName;         \textcolor{comment}{// Pointer to owner window's name for debugging}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2439     \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_draw_vert}{ImDrawVert}}*             \_VtxWritePtr;       \textcolor{comment}{// [Internal] point within VtxBuffer.Data after each add command (to avoid using the ImVector<> operators too much)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2440     ImDrawIdx*              \_IdxWritePtr;       \textcolor{comment}{// [Internal] point within IdxBuffer.Data after each add command (to avoid using the ImVector<> operators too much)}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2643 \textcolor{comment}{// Flags for ImFontAtlas build}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2644 \textcolor{keyword}{enum} ImFontAtlasFlags\_}
\DoxyCodeLine{2645 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2646     ImFontAtlasFlags\_None               = 0,}
\DoxyCodeLine{2647     ImFontAtlasFlags\_NoPowerOfTwoHeight = 1 << 0,   \textcolor{comment}{// Don't round the height to next power of two}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2648     ImFontAtlasFlags\_NoMouseCursors     = 1 << 1,   \textcolor{comment}{// Don't build software mouse cursors into the atlas (save a little texture memory)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2649     ImFontAtlasFlags\_NoBakedLines       = 1 << 2    \textcolor{comment}{// Don't build thick line textures into the atlas (save a little texture memory). The AntiAliasedLinesUseTex features uses them, otherwise they will be rendered using polygons (more expensive for CPU/GPU).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2650 \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{2651 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2652 \textcolor{comment}{// Load and rasterize multiple TTF/OTF fonts into a same texture. The font atlas will build a single texture holding:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2653 \textcolor{comment}{//  -\/ One or more fonts.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2654 \textcolor{comment}{//  -\/ Custom graphics data needed to render the shapes needed by Dear ImGui.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2655 \textcolor{comment}{//  -\/ Mouse cursor shapes for software cursor rendering (unless setting 'Flags |= ImFontAtlasFlags\_NoMouseCursors' in the font atlas).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2656 \textcolor{comment}{// It is the user-\/code responsibility to set\_appData/build the atlas, then upload the pixel data into a texture accessible by your graphics api.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2657 \textcolor{comment}{//  -\/ Optionally, call any of the AddFont*** functions. If you don't call any, the default font embedded in the code will be loaded for you.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2658 \textcolor{comment}{//  -\/ Call GetTexDataAsAlpha8() or GetTexDataAsRGBA32() to build and retrieve pixels data.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2659 \textcolor{comment}{//  -\/ Upload the pixels data into a texture within your graphics system (see imgui\_impl\_xxxx.cpp examples)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2660 \textcolor{comment}{//  -\/ Call SetTexID(my\_tex\_id); and pass the pointer/identifier to your texture in a format natural to your graphics API.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2661 \textcolor{comment}{//    This value will be passed back to you during rendering to identify the texture. Read FAQ entry about ImTextureID for more details.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2662 \textcolor{comment}{// Common pitfalls:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2663 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ If you pass a 'glyph\_ranges' array to AddFont*** functions, you need to make sure that your array persist up until the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2664 \textcolor{comment}{//   atlas is build (when calling GetTexData*** or Build()). We only copy the pointer, not the data.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2665 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Important: By default, AddFontFromMemoryTTF() takes ownership of the data. Even though we are not writing to it, we will free the pointer on destruction.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2666 \textcolor{comment}{//   You can set font\_cfg-\/>FontDataOwnedByAtlas=false to keep ownership of your data and it won't be freed,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2667 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Even though many functions are suffixed with "{}TTF"{}, OTF data is supported just as well.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2668 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ This is an old API and it is currently awkward for those and and various other reasons! We will address them in the future!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2669 \textcolor{keyword}{struct }\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_font_atlas}{ImFontAtlas}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2670 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2671     IMGUI\_API \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_font_atlas}{ImFontAtlas}}();}
\DoxyCodeLine{2672     IMGUI\_API \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_font_atlas}{\string~ImFontAtlas}}();}
\DoxyCodeLine{2673     IMGUI\_API \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_font}{ImFont}}*           AddFont(\textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_font_config}{ImFontConfig}}* font\_cfg);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2674     IMGUI\_API \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_font}{ImFont}}*           AddFontDefault(\textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_font_config}{ImFontConfig}}* font\_cfg = NULL);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2675     IMGUI\_API \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_font}{ImFont}}*           AddFontFromFileTTF(\textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}* filename, \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} size\_pixels, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_font_config}{ImFontConfig}}* font\_cfg = NULL, \textcolor{keyword}{const} ImWchar* glyph\_ranges = NULL);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2676     IMGUI\_API \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_font}{ImFont}}*           AddFontFromMemoryTTF(\textcolor{keywordtype}{void}* font\_data, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} font\_size, \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} size\_pixels, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_font_config}{ImFontConfig}}* font\_cfg = NULL, \textcolor{keyword}{const} ImWchar* glyph\_ranges = NULL); \textcolor{comment}{// Note: Transfer ownership of 'ttf\_data' to ImFontAtlas! Will be deleted after destruction of the atlas. Set font\_cfg-\/>FontDataOwnedByAtlas=false to keep ownership of your data and it won't be freed.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2677     IMGUI\_API \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_font}{ImFont}}*           AddFontFromMemoryCompressedTTF(\textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}* compressed\_font\_data, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} compressed\_font\_size, \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} size\_pixels, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_font_config}{ImFontConfig}}* font\_cfg = NULL, \textcolor{keyword}{const} ImWchar* glyph\_ranges = NULL); \textcolor{comment}{// 'compressed\_font\_data' still owned by caller. Compress with binary\_to\_compressed\_c.cpp with -\/base85 parameter.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2679     IMGUI\_API \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}              ClearInputData();           \textcolor{comment}{// Clear input data (all ImFontConfig structures including sizes, TTF data, glyph ranges, etc.) = all the data used to build the texture and fonts.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2680     IMGUI\_API \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}              ClearTexData();             \textcolor{comment}{// Clear output texture data (CPU side). Saves RAM once the texture has been copied to graphics memory.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2681     IMGUI\_API \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}              ClearFonts();               \textcolor{comment}{// Clear output font data (glyphs storage, UV coordinates).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2682     IMGUI\_API \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}              Clear();                    \textcolor{comment}{// Clear all input and output.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2683 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2684     \textcolor{comment}{// Build atlas, retrieve pixel data.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2685     \textcolor{comment}{// User is in charge of copying the pixels into graphics memory (e.g. create a texture with your engine). Then store your texture handle with SetTexID().}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2686     \textcolor{comment}{// The pitch is always = Width * BytesPerPixels (1 or 4)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2687     \textcolor{comment}{// Building in RGBA32 format is provided for convenience and compatibility, but note that unless you manually manipulate or copy color data into}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2688     \textcolor{comment}{// the texture (e.g. when using the AddCustomRect*** api), then the RGB pixels emitted will always be white (\string~75\% of memory/bandwidth waste.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2689     IMGUI\_API \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool}              Build();                    \textcolor{comment}{// Build pixels data. This is called automatically for you by the GetTexData*** functions.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2690     IMGUI\_API \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}              GetTexDataAsAlpha8(\textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}** out\_pixels, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}* out\_width, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}* out\_height, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}* out\_bytes\_per\_pixel = NULL);  \textcolor{comment}{// 1 byte per-\/pixel}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2691     IMGUI\_API \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}              GetTexDataAsRGBA32(\textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}** out\_pixels, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}* out\_width, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}* out\_height, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}* out\_bytes\_per\_pixel = NULL);  \textcolor{comment}{// 4 bytes-\/per-\/pixel}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2692     \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool}                        IsBuilt()\textcolor{keyword}{ const             }\{ \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} Fonts.Size > 0 \&\& (TexPixelsAlpha8 != NULL || TexPixelsRGBA32 != NULL); \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2715     \textcolor{comment}{// You can request arbitrary rectangles to be packed into the atlas, for your own purposes.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2716     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ After calling Build(), you can query the rectangle position and render your pixels.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2717     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ If you render colored output, set 'atlas-\/>TexPixelsUseColors = true' as this may help some backends decide of prefered texture format.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2718     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ You can also request your rectangles to be mapped as font glyph (given a font + Unicode point),}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2719     \textcolor{comment}{//   so you can render e.g. custom colorful icons and use them as regular glyphs.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2720     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Read docs/FONTS.md for more details about using colorful icons.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2721     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Note: this API may be redesigned later in order to support multi-\/monitor varying DPI settings.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2825 \textcolor{comment}{// Flags stored in ImGuiViewport::Flags, giving indications to the platform backends.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2826 \textcolor{keyword}{enum} ImGuiViewportFlags\_}
\DoxyCodeLine{2827 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2828     ImGuiViewportFlags\_None                     = 0,}
\DoxyCodeLine{2829     ImGuiViewportFlags\_IsPlatformWindow         = 1 << 0,   \textcolor{comment}{// Represent a Platform Window}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2830     ImGuiViewportFlags\_IsPlatformMonitor        = 1 << 1,   \textcolor{comment}{// Represent a Platform Monitor (unused yet)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2831     ImGuiViewportFlags\_OwnedByApp               = 1 << 2,   \textcolor{comment}{// Platform Window: is created/managed by the application (rather than a dear imgui backend)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2832     ImGuiViewportFlags\_NoDecoration             = 1 << 3,   \textcolor{comment}{// Platform Window: Disable platform decorations: title bar, borders, etc. (generally set all windows, but if ImGuiConfigFlags\_ViewportsDecoration is set we only set this on popups/tooltips)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2833     ImGuiViewportFlags\_NoTaskBarIcon            = 1 << 4,   \textcolor{comment}{// Platform Window: Disable platform task bar icon (generally set on popups/tooltips, or all windows if ImGuiConfigFlags\_ViewportsNoTaskBarIcon is set)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2834     ImGuiViewportFlags\_NoFocusOnAppearing       = 1 << 5,   \textcolor{comment}{// Platform Window: Don't take focus when created.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2835     ImGuiViewportFlags\_NoFocusOnClick           = 1 << 6,   \textcolor{comment}{// Platform Window: Don't take focus when clicked on.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2836     ImGuiViewportFlags\_NoInputs                 = 1 << 7,   \textcolor{comment}{// Platform Window: Make mouse pass through so we can drag this window while peaking behind it.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2837     ImGuiViewportFlags\_NoRendererClear          = 1 << 8,   \textcolor{comment}{// Platform Window: Renderer doesn't need to clear the framebuffer ahead (because we will fill it entirely).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2838     ImGuiViewportFlags\_TopMost                  = 1 << 9,   \textcolor{comment}{// Platform Window: Display on top (for tooltips only).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2839     ImGuiViewportFlags\_Minimized                = 1 << 10,  \textcolor{comment}{// Platform Window: Window is minimized, can skip render. When minimized we tend to avoid using the viewport pos/size for clipping window or testing if they are contained in the viewport.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2840     ImGuiViewportFlags\_NoAutoMerge              = 1 << 11,  \textcolor{comment}{// Platform Window: Avoid merging this window into another host window. This can only be set via ImGuiWindowClass viewport flags override (because we need to now ahead if we are going to create a viewport in the first place!).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2841     ImGuiViewportFlags\_CanHostOtherWindows      = 1 << 12   \textcolor{comment}{// Main viewport: can host multiple imgui windows (secondary viewports are associated to a single window).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2842 \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{2843 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2844 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Currently represents the Platform Window created by the application which is hosting our Dear ImGui windows.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2845 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ With multi-\/viewport enabled, we extend this concept to have multiple active viewports.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2846 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ In the future we will extend this concept further to also represent Platform Monitor and support a "{}no main platform window"{} operation mode.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2847 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ About Main Area vs Work Area:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2848 \textcolor{comment}{//   -\/ Main Area = entire viewport.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2849 \textcolor{comment}{//   -\/ Work Area = entire viewport minus sections used by main menu bars (for platform windows), or by task bar (for platform monitor).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2850 \textcolor{comment}{//   -\/ Windows are generally trying to stay within the Work Area of their host viewport.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2851 \textcolor{keyword}{struct }\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_gui_viewport}{ImGuiViewport}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2852 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2853     ImGuiID             ID;                     \textcolor{comment}{// Unique identifier for the viewport}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2854     ImGuiViewportFlags  Flags;                  \textcolor{comment}{// See ImGuiViewportFlags\_}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2855     \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_vec2}{ImVec2}}              Pos;                    \textcolor{comment}{// Main Area: Position of the viewport (Dear ImGui coordinates are the same as OS desktop/native coordinates)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2856     \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_vec2}{ImVec2}}              Size;                   \textcolor{comment}{// Main Area: Size of the viewport.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2857     \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_vec2}{ImVec2}}              WorkPos;                \textcolor{comment}{// Work Area: Position of the viewport minus task bars, menus bars, status bars (>= Pos)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2858     \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_vec2}{ImVec2}}              WorkSize;               \textcolor{comment}{// Work Area: Size of the viewport minus task bars, menu bars, status bars (<= Size)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2859     \textcolor{keywordtype}{float}               DpiScale;               \textcolor{comment}{// 1.0f = 96 DPI = No extra scale.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2860     ImGuiID             ParentViewportId;       \textcolor{comment}{// (Advanced) 0: no parent. Instruct the platform backend to set\_appData a parent/child relationship between platform windows.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2861     \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_draw_data}{ImDrawData}}*         DrawData;               \textcolor{comment}{// The ImDrawData corresponding to this viewport. Valid after Render() and until the next call to NewFrame().}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2862 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2863     \textcolor{comment}{// Our design separate the Renderer and Platform backends to facilitate combining default backends with each others.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2864     \textcolor{comment}{// When our create your own backend for a custom engine, it is possible that both Renderer and Platform will be handled}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2865     \textcolor{comment}{// by the same system and you may not need to use all the UserData/Handle fields.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2866     \textcolor{comment}{// The library never uses those fields, they are merely storage to facilitate backend implementation.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2867     \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}*               RendererUserData;       \textcolor{comment}{// void* to hold custom data structure for the renderer (e.g. swap chain, framebuffers etc.). generally set by your Renderer\_CreateWindow function.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2868     \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}*               PlatformUserData;       \textcolor{comment}{// void* to hold custom data structure for the OS / platform (e.g. windowing info, render context). generally set by your Platform\_CreateWindow function.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2869     \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}*               PlatformHandle;         \textcolor{comment}{// void* for FindViewportByPlatformHandle(). (e.g. suggested to use natural platform handle such as HWND, GLFWWindow*, SDL\_Window*)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2870     \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}*               PlatformHandleRaw;      \textcolor{comment}{// void* to hold lower-\/level, platform-\/native window handle (e.g. the HWND) when using an abstraction layer like GLFW or SDL (where PlatformHandle would be a SDL\_Window*)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2871     \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool}                PlatformRequestMove;    \textcolor{comment}{// Platform window requested move (e.g. window was moved by the OS / host window manager, authoritative position will be OS window position)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2872     \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool}                PlatformRequestResize;  \textcolor{comment}{// Platform window requested resize (e.g. window was resized by the OS / host window manager, authoritative size will be OS window size)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2873     \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool}                PlatformRequestClose;   \textcolor{comment}{// Platform window requested closure (e.g. window was moved by the OS / host window manager, e.g. pressing ALT-\/F4)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2874 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2875     \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_gui_viewport}{ImGuiViewport}}()     \{ memset(\textcolor{keyword}{this}, 0, \textcolor{keyword}{sizeof}(*\textcolor{keyword}{this})); \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2876     \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_gui_viewport}{\string~ImGuiViewport}}()    \{ IM\_ASSERT(PlatformUserData == NULL \&\& RendererUserData == NULL); \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2877 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2878     \textcolor{comment}{// Helpers}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2879     \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_vec2}{ImVec2}}              GetCenter()\textcolor{keyword}{ const       }\{ \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_vec2}{ImVec2}}(Pos.x + Size.x * 0.5f, Pos.y + Size.y * 0.5f); \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2880     \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_vec2}{ImVec2}}              GetWorkCenter()\textcolor{keyword}{ const   }\{ \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_vec2}{ImVec2}}(WorkPos.x + WorkSize.x * 0.5f, WorkPos.y + WorkSize.y * 0.5f); \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2881 \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{2882 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2883 \textcolor{comment}{//-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2884 \textcolor{comment}{// [SECTION] Platform interface for multi-\/viewport support}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2885 \textcolor{comment}{//-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2886 \textcolor{comment}{// [BETA] (Optional) This is completely optional, for advanced users!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2887 \textcolor{comment}{// If you are new to Dear ImGui and trying to integrate it into your engine, you can probably ignore this for now.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2888 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2889 \textcolor{comment}{// This feature allows you to seamlessly drag Dear ImGui windows outside of your application viewport.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2890 \textcolor{comment}{// This is achieved by creating new Platform/OS windows on the fly, and rendering into them.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2891 \textcolor{comment}{// Dear ImGui manages the viewport structures, and the backend create and maintain one Platform/OS window for each of those viewports.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2892 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2893 \textcolor{comment}{// See Glossary https://github.com/ocornut/imgui/wiki/Glossary for details about some of the terminology.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2894 \textcolor{comment}{// See Thread https://github.com/ocornut/imgui/issues/1542 for gifs, news and questions about this evolving feature.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2895 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2896 \textcolor{comment}{// About the coordinates system:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2897 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ When multi-\/viewports are enabled, all Dear ImGui coordinates become absolute coordinates (same as OS coordinates!)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2898 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ So e.g. ImGui::SetNextWindowPos(ImVec2(0,0)) will position a window relative to your primary monitor!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2899 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ If you want to position windows relative to your main application viewport, use ImGui::GetMainViewport()-\/>Pos as a base position.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2900 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2901 \textcolor{comment}{// Steps to use multi-\/viewports in your application, when using a default backend from the examples/ folder:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2902 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Application:  Enable feature with 'io.ConfigFlags |= ImGuiConfigFlags\_ViewportsEnable'.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2903 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Backend:      The backend initialization will set\_appData all necessary ImGuiPlatformIO's functions and update monitors info every frame.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2904 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Application:  In your main loop, call ImGui::UpdatePlatformWindows(), ImGui::RenderPlatformWindowsDefault() after EndFrame() or Render().}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2905 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Application:  Fix absolute coordinates used in ImGui::SetWindowPos() or ImGui::SetNextWindowPos() calls.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2906 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2907 \textcolor{comment}{// Steps to use multi-\/viewports in your application, when using a custom backend:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2908 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Important:    THIS IS NOT EASY TO DO and comes with many subtleties not described here!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2909 \textcolor{comment}{//                 It's also an experimental feature, so some of the requirements may evolve.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2910 \textcolor{comment}{//                 Consider using default backends if you can. Either way, carefully follow and refer to examples/ backends for details.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2911 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Application:  Enable feature with 'io.ConfigFlags |= ImGuiConfigFlags\_ViewportsEnable'.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2912 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Backend:      Hook ImGuiPlatformIO's Platform\_* and Renderer\_* callbacks (see below).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2913 \textcolor{comment}{//                 Set 'io.BackendFlags |= ImGuiBackendFlags\_PlatformHasViewports' and 'io.BackendFlags |= ImGuiBackendFlags\_PlatformHasViewports'.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2914 \textcolor{comment}{//                 Update ImGuiPlatformIO's Monitors list every frame.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2915 \textcolor{comment}{//                 Update MousePos every frame, in absolute coordinates.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2916 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Application:  In your main loop, call ImGui::UpdatePlatformWindows(), ImGui::RenderPlatformWindowsDefault() after EndFrame() or Render().}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2917 \textcolor{comment}{//                 You may skip calling RenderPlatformWindowsDefault() if its API is not convenient for your needs. Read comments below.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2918 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Application:  Fix absolute coordinates used in ImGui::SetWindowPos() or ImGui::SetNextWindowPos() calls.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2919 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2920 \textcolor{comment}{// About ImGui::RenderPlatformWindowsDefault():}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2921 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ This function is a mostly a \_helper\_ for the common-\/most cases, and to facilitate using default backends.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2922 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ You can check its simple source code to understand what it does.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2923 \textcolor{comment}{//   It basically iterates secondary viewports and call 4 functions that are set\_appData in ImGuiPlatformIO, if available:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2924 \textcolor{comment}{//     Platform\_RenderWindow(), Renderer\_RenderWindow(), Platform\_SwapBuffers(), Renderer\_SwapBuffers()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2925 \textcolor{comment}{//   Those functions pointers exists only for the benefit of RenderPlatformWindowsDefault().}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2926 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ If you have very specific rendering needs (e.g. flipping multiple swap-\/chain simultaneously, unusual sync/threading issues, etc.),}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2927 \textcolor{comment}{//   you may be tempted to ignore RenderPlatformWindowsDefault() and write customized code to perform your renderingg.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2928 \textcolor{comment}{//   You may decide to set\_appData the platform\_io's *RenderWindow and *SwapBuffers pointers and call your functions through those pointers,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2929 \textcolor{comment}{//   or you may decide to never set\_appData those pointers and call your code directly. They are a convenience, not an obligatory interface.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2930 \textcolor{comment}{//-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2931 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2932 \textcolor{comment}{// (Optional) Access via ImGui::GetPlatformIO()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2933 \textcolor{keyword}{struct }\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_gui_platform_i_o}{ImGuiPlatformIO}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2934 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2935     \textcolor{comment}{//-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2936     \textcolor{comment}{// Input -\/ Backend interface/functions + Monitor List}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2937     \textcolor{comment}{//-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2938 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2939     \textcolor{comment}{// (Optional) Platform functions (e.g. Win32, GLFW, SDL2)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2940     \textcolor{comment}{// For reference, the second column shows which function are generally calling the Platform Functions:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2941     \textcolor{comment}{//   N = ImGui::NewFrame()                        \string~ beginning of the dear imgui frame: read info from platform/OS windows (latest size/position)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2942     \textcolor{comment}{//   F = ImGui::Begin(), ImGui::EndFrame()        \string~ during the dear imgui frame}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2943     \textcolor{comment}{//   U = ImGui::UpdatePlatformWindows()           \string~ after the dear imgui frame: create and update all platform/OS windows}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2944     \textcolor{comment}{//   R = ImGui::RenderPlatformWindowsDefault()    \string~ render}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2945     \textcolor{comment}{//   D = ImGui::DestroyPlatformWindows()          \string~ shutdown}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2946     \textcolor{comment}{// The general idea is that NewFrame() we will read the current Platform/OS state, and UpdatePlatformWindows() will write to it.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2947     \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2948     \textcolor{comment}{// The functions are designed so we can mix and match 2 imgui\_impl\_xxxx files, one for the Platform (\string~window/input handling), one for Renderer.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2949     \textcolor{comment}{// Custom engine backends will often provide both Platform and Renderer interfaces and so may not need to use all functions.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2950     \textcolor{comment}{// Platform functions are typically called before their Renderer counterpart, apart from Destroy which are called the other way.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2951 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2952     \textcolor{comment}{// Platform function -\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/ Called by -\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2989     \textcolor{comment}{// Viewports list (the list is updated by calling ImGui::EndFrame or ImGui::Render)}}
